jame monro born april westmoreland counti Va He
son spenc monro elizabeth jone nativ virginia
when eighteenth year enlist privat soldier
armi fight independ sever battl wound
engag trenton promot rank captain
infantri dure act aid lord stirl
distinguish He studi law direct thoma
jefferson governor virginia appoint visit
armi south carolina import mission In
elect virginia assembl counti king georg
bodi chosen member execut council the next year
chosen deleg continent congress remain
member member marri miss kortright new
york citi retir congress began practic law
fredericksburg va elect legislatur In
deleg state convent assembl consid feder
constitut wa senat virginia In may
appoint washington minist franc He recal
elect legislatur In elect
governor virginia In appoint presid jefferson envoy
extraordinari franc sent london successor
rufu king In perform diplomat mission spain
relat boundari louisiana return london follow
year return unit state In elect
governor state year resign offic
becom secretari state presid madison after captur
washington appoint war depart
posit held without relinquish offic
secretari state He remain head depart state
close mr madison term wa elect presid
reelect retir march resid
loudoun counti Va In elect member convent
call revis constitut state unanim
